Top 32 Decklists
================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on March 6, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/walkinshaw.jpg)
By Ray “blisterguy” Walkinshaw











Some players got so close, but finished just outside of the Top 8. Nonetheless, Top 32 is an impressive feat at a Grand Prix, and you can take a look at what these players brought with them for yourself.







#### James Storey – R/G Tron – GP Melbourne – 37 points


##### 




![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
